| <span data-ttu-id="ea9da-1518">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ea9da-1518">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ea9da-1519">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ea9da-1519">Value</span></span> |
